issued a press release announcing its unaudited financial results for the quarter ended March 31, 2022. A copy of the press release making
the announcement is attached as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, and shall
not be incorporated by reference into any registration statement or other document filed under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended
(the &#8220;Securities Act&#8221;), or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing.</span></p>

<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="text-align: right; margin: 0"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center; background-color: white"><B>IT Tech Packaging,
Inc. Announces First Quarter 2022 Unaudited Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">BAODING,&nbsp;China,&nbsp;May
10 2022&nbsp;/PRNewswire/ &ndash;&nbsp;IT Tech Packaging, Inc. (NYSE American: ITP) (&ldquo;IT Tech Packaging&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;),
a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products in&nbsp;North China, today announced its unaudited financial results
for the first&nbsp;quarter ended&nbsp;March 31, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Mr. Zhenyong Liu, Chairman
and Chief Executive Officer of the Company, commented, &ldquo;In the first quarter of 2022, our business was significantly affected by
the dynamic and challenging macro environment and resurgence of COVID-19. We have resumed our business operation, and we expect to actively
improve our business plans and launch a series of initiatives to optimize our revenue structure and diversify our business to counter
the adverse effects of COVID-19 and the governmental policy developments on our operations and financial results. Looking forward, we
believe our business fundamentals will defend our leading position in the industry and we remain intently focused on ramping production,broadening
the market, and driving long-term value for shareholders in 2022 and beyond.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>First Quarter
2022 Unaudited Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Revenue</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">For the first quarter
of 2022, total revenue decreased by 36.1%, to&nbsp;approximately $15.48 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $24.21 million&nbsp;for the
same period of last year. The decrease in total revenue was mainly due to the decrease in sales volume of regular CMP, offset printing
paper and tissue paper products.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">The following table summarizes
revenue, volume and ASP by product for the first quarter of 2022 and 2021, respectively:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from CMP, including both regular CMP and
light-Weight CMP, decreased by 27.5%, to&nbsp;approximately $15.03 million&nbsp;and accounted for 97.1% of total revenue for the first
quarter of 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $20.71 million, or 85.6% of total revenue for the same period of last year. The Company
sold 29,086 tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$517/tonne in the first quarter of 2022, compared to 41,296&nbsp;tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$502/tonne
in the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Of the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP
decreased by 22.8%, to&nbsp;approximately $13.10 million for the first quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $16.96
million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 25,245 tonnes of regular CMPat an ASP of&nbsp;$519/tonne during the first quarter
of 2022, compared to 33,626 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$504/tonne for the same period of last year. Revenue from light-weight CMP decreased
by 48.6%, to&nbsp;approximately $1.93 million for the first quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $3.75 million for
the same period of last year. The Company sold 3,841 tonnes of light-weight CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$502/tonne for the first quarter of
2022, compared to 7,670 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$489/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from offset printing paper was nil &nbsp;for
the first quarter of 2022, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately&nbsp;$2.12 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The Company
sold 3,142 tonnes of offset printing paper at an ASP of&nbsp;$673/tonne in the first quarter of 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from tissue paper
products decreased by 68.2%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.40 million for the first quarter of 2022, from&nbsp;approximately&nbsp;$1.25 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year. The Company sold 397 tonnes of tissue paper products at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,003/tonne for the first quarter
of 2022, compared to 1,120 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,117/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from face masks
decreased by 56.6%, to&nbsp;approximately $56,596&nbsp;for the first quarter ended&nbsp;March 31, 2022, from $130,458 for the same period
of last year. The Company sold 3,014 thousand pieces of face masks for the first quarter of2022, compared to 3,836 thousand pieces of
face masks for the same period oflast year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2; Options: NewSection; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Gross Profit and Gross
Margin</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total cost of sales decreased by 32.2%, to&nbsp;approximately
$15.17 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2022 from&nbsp;approximately $22.38 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The decrease
in overall cost of sales was mainly due to the decrease in sales quantity of regular CMP, offset printing paper and tissue paper products.&nbsp;
Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, and tissue paper products were&nbsp;$491,&nbsp;$461,$nil
and&nbsp;$2,424, respectively, for the first quarter of 2022, compared to $462,&nbsp;$435,&nbsp;$543&nbsp;and&nbsp;$1,525, respectively,
for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total gross profit was&nbsp;approximately $0.31
million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2022, compare to the gross profit of&nbsp;approximately $1.83 million&nbsp;for the same period of
last year as a result of factors described above. Overall gross margin was 2.0% for the first quarter of 2022, compared to 7.6% for the
same period of last year. Gross profit(loss) margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, tissue paper products and
face mask products were 5.4%, 8.2%, nil%, -141.5% and 29.5%, respectively, for the first quarter of 2022, compared to 8.5%, 10.9%, 19.4%,
-36.5% and 18.8%, respectively, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Selling, General and
Administrative Expenses</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Selling, general and
administrative expenses (&ldquo;SG&amp;A&rdquo;) increased by 29.2%, to&nbsp;approximately $3.30 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2022
from&nbsp;approximately $2.56 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Loss from Operations</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Loss from operations
was&nbsp;approximately $2.96 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2022, a decrease of 308.2%, from loss from operations of&nbsp;approximately
$0.72 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Operating loss margin was 19.1% for the first quarter of 2022, compared to operating
loss margin of 3.0% for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Net Loss</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Net loss was&nbsp;approximately
$2.49 million, or loss per share of $0.03, compared to net loss of&nbsp;approximately $4.34 million, or loss per share of $0.12, for the
same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>EBITDA</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">EBITDA was&nbsp;approximately
$1.20 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately negative $0.07 million&nbsp;for the same period of last
year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Note 1: Non-GAAP Financial
Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">In addition to our U.S.
GAAP results, this press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the Securities and Exchange
Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;). The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation and amortization. EBITDA
is a key measure used by management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes this measure is useful to
investors because it is an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations, the Company&rsquo;s presentation
of EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed as an alternative to measures
of financial performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>Cash, Liquidity and
Financial Position</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">As of&nbsp;March 31, 2022, the Company had cash
and bank balances, short-term debt (including bank loans, current portion of long-term loans from credit union and related party loans),
and long-term debt (including related party loans) of&nbsp;approximately $15.36 million,&nbsp;$13.58 million and&nbsp;$2.99 million, respectively,
compared to &nbsp;approximately $11.20&nbsp;million,&nbsp;$13.52&nbsp;million and&nbsp;$2.98 million, respectively, as of&nbsp;December
31, 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Net accounts receivable
was&nbsp;approximately $4.98&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;March 31, 2022, compared to approximately&nbsp;$4.87&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;December
31, 2021. Net inventory was approximately&nbsp;$4.35&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;March 31, 2022, compared to&nbsp;approximately $5.84&nbsp;million
as of&nbsp;December 31, 2021. As of&nbsp;March 31, 2022, the Company had current assets of&nbsp;approximately $48.62&nbsp;million and
current liabilities of&nbsp;approximately $19.94 million, resulting in a working capital of&nbsp;approximately $28.68&nbsp;million. This
was compared to current assets of approximately $55.52 million and current liabilities of approximately $20.43 million, resulting in a
working capital of approximately $35.09 million as of&nbsp;December 31, 2021.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Net cash provided by operating activities was&nbsp;approximately
$4.41 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2022, compared to net cash used in operating activities of approximately&nbsp;$8.28 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year. Net cash used in investing activities was&nbsp;approximately $7.18 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of
2022, compared to approximately $0.04 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Net cash provided by financing activities was&nbsp;approximately
$6.89 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2022, compared to approximately $41.79 million for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><B>About IT Tech Packaging,
Inc.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Founded in 1996, IT Tech
Packaging, Inc. is a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products and single-use face masks in&nbsp;North China.
Using recycled paper as its primary raw material (with the exception of its tissue paper products), ITP produces and distributes three
categories of paper products: corrugating medium paper, offset printing paper and tissue paper products. With production based in Baoding
and Xingtai in&nbsp;North China&rsquo;s&nbsp;Hebei Province, ITP is located strategically close to the&nbsp;Beijing&nbsp;and&nbsp;Tianjin&nbsp;region,
home to a growing base of industrial and manufacturing activities and one of the largest markets for paper products consumption in the
country. ITP has been listed on the NYSE American since&nbsp;December 2009. For more information, please visit:&nbsp;http://www.itpackaging.cn/.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>
